## PHASE: P7 both-sides composer (#1156) — DIFF gate iter 1 (brief in parallel review). PURE composer only (wiring into the report assembler + UI deferred to I-cred-007b). compose_both_sides(contradiction_edges, weight_mass, claims) -> list[BothSidesBlock]: maps each Phase-5 ContradictionEdge's two claim_cluster_ids to their Phase-6 weight_mass + independent_origin_count + Phase-5 evidence_ids; sides ordered by weight_mass DESC (discloses which side has more evidence weight, NEVER asserts which is true); the LOW-weight side is KEPT, never dropped (operator Decision 2); missing weight -> 0.0/0 fail-soft. render_both_sides -> NEUTRAL markdown ('' for [] = default-OFF byte-identity); a guardrail test asserts NONE of {fringe,misinformation,debunked,conspiracy,warning,unreliable,false claim,discredited}. diff --git a/src/polaris_graph/synthesis/both_sides.py b/src/polaris_graph/synthesis/both_sides.py

```diff
+++ b/src/polaris_graph/synthesis/both_sides.py
@@ -0,0 +1,158 @@
+"""I-cred-007 (Phase 7, L6) — NEUTRAL both-sides disclosure composer (pure module).
+
+For a CONTESTED claim (a claim-cluster pair joined by a Phase-5 ``ContradictionEdge``), compose a
+NEUTRAL both-sides disclosure: each side shown as a LEGITIMATE position with its transparent evidence
+weight (Phase-6 origin-cluster ``weight_mass``), its independent-origin count, and its cited
+``evidence_id``s — in neutral language, ALWAYS visible. The user judges; POLARIS discloses the weight
+behind each side honestly rather than labelling one "true" or "fringe" (operator Decision 2, plan §9.3).
+
+POSTURE (binding):
+  * ADVISORY / DISCLOSURE ONLY. This is a SEPARATE block (rendered like ``limitations_text``), appended
+    AFTER verified prose. It NEVER edits verified sentences, NEVER runs inside ``strict_verify``, NEVER
+    touches the 4-role D8 release gate. strict_verify's six checks stay the only binding faithfulness gate.
+  * NEUTRAL framing: no "fringe / misinformation / warning / debunked / conspiracy / unreliable" labels.
+  * DEFAULT-OFF byte-identical: ``PG_SWEEP_BOTHSIDES_DISCLOSURE`` (no production caller; pure library).
+  * Weight is the Phase-6 origin-cluster ``weight_mass`` (authority of independent canonical origins),
+    never headcount. Both sides get their honest weight; the LOW-weight side is shown, not dropped.
+  * PURE: no input mutation, no network, no faithfulness-file import; LAW VI; snake_case.
+
+This issue ships the pure composer ONLY; wiring the rendered block into the report assembler + the UI
+affordance is a separate step (I-cred-007b), keeping this faithfulness-safe and default-OFF.
+"""
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import os
+from dataclasses import dataclass
+from typing import Any
+
+_FLAG = "PG_SWEEP_BOTHSIDES_DISCLOSURE"
+_OFF_VALUES = frozenset({"", "0", "false", "off", "no"})
+
+
+def bothsides_disclosure_enabled() -> bool:
+    """True unless ``PG_SWEEP_BOTHSIDES_DISCLOSURE`` is unset/falsey (default OFF => byte-identical)."""
+    return os.environ.get(_FLAG, "").strip().lower() not in _OFF_VALUES
+
+
+def _num(value: Any) -> float:
+    try:
+        x = float(value)
+    except (TypeError, ValueError):
+        return 0.0
+    return 0.0 if (x != x or x in (float("inf"), float("-inf"))) else x
+
+
+@dataclass
+class SidePosition:
+    """One side of a contested claim, with its transparent evidence weight."""
+
+    claim_cluster_id: str
+    subject: str
+    predicate: str
+    weight_mass: float            # Phase-6 origin-cluster weight-mass behind this side
+    independent_origin_count: int
+    evidence_ids: tuple           # the cited evidence for this side (one-click span access)
+
+
+@dataclass
+class BothSidesBlock:
+    """A contested topic + its 2+ positions, ordered by evidence weight (NOT by "correctness")."""
+
+    subject: str
+    sides: list
+    source: str                   # which detector raised the contradiction (numeric/qualitative/semantic)
+    severity: str
+
+
+def compose_both_sides(
+    contradiction_edges: list,
+    weight_mass: list,
+    claims: list,
+) -> list[BothSidesBlock]:
+    """Compose one BothSidesBlock per contradiction edge — pure, no input mutation.
+
+    Maps each ``ContradictionEdge``'s two ``claim_cluster_ids`` to their Phase-6 ``ClaimWeightMass``
+    (weight + independent-origin count) and Phase-5 ``AtomicClaim`` info (subject/predicate/evidence_ids).
+    Sides are ordered by ``weight_mass`` DESC — disclosing which side has MORE evidence weight, never
+    asserting which is true; the low-weight side is kept, never dropped. A missing weight defaults to
+    0.0 / 0 (fail-soft disclosure, never a crash, never a fabricated weight).
+    """
+    weight_by_cluster: dict[str, Any] = {}
+    for cwm in (weight_mass or []):
+        ccid = str(getattr(cwm, "claim_cluster_id", "") or "")
+        if ccid:
+            weight_by_cluster[ccid] = cwm
+
+    info: dict[str, dict[str, Any]] = {}
+    for claim in (claims or []):
+        ccid = str(getattr(claim, "claim_cluster_id", "") or "")
+        if not ccid:
+            continue
+        rec = info.setdefault(ccid, {"subject": "", "predicate": "", "evidence_ids": set()})
+        if not rec["subject"]:
+            rec["subject"] = str(getattr(claim, "subject", "") or "")
+        if not rec["predicate"]:
+            rec["predicate"] = str(getattr(claim, "predicate", "") or "")
+        eid = str(getattr(claim, "evidence_id", "") or "")
+        if eid:
+            rec["evidence_ids"].add(eid)
+
+    blocks: list[BothSidesBlock] = []
+    for edge in (contradiction_edges or []):
+        cluster_ids = tuple(getattr(edge, "claim_cluster_ids", ()) or ())
+        if len(cluster_ids) < 2:
+            continue  # a both-sides block needs two distinct positions
+        sides: list[SidePosition] = []
+        for raw_ccid in cluster_ids:
+            ccid = str(raw_ccid)
+            cwm = weight_by_cluster.get(ccid)
+            rec = info.get(ccid, {})
+            sides.append(SidePosition(
+                claim_cluster_id=ccid,
+                subject=str(rec.get("subject", "") or getattr(edge, "subject", "") or ""),
+                predicate=str(rec.get("predicate", "") or getattr(edge, "predicate", "") or ""),
+                weight_mass=_num(getattr(cwm, "weight_mass", 0.0)) if cwm is not None else 0.0,
+                independent_origin_count=(
+                    int(getattr(cwm, "independent_origin_count", 0) or 0) if cwm is not None else 0
+                ),
+                evidence_ids=tuple(sorted(rec.get("evidence_ids", set()))),
+            ))
+        # Order by weight DESC; stable claim_cluster_id tiebreak for determinism. This discloses which
+        # side carries more independent-origin evidence weight — it does NOT assert which is correct.
+        sides.sort(key=lambda s: (-s.weight_mass, s.claim_cluster_id))
+        blocks.append(BothSidesBlock(
+            subject=str(getattr(edge, "subject", "") or (sides[0].subject if sides else "")),
+            sides=sides,
+            source=str(getattr(edge, "source", "") or ""),
+            severity=str(getattr(edge, "severity", "") or "review"),
+        ))
+    return blocks
+
+
+def render_both_sides(blocks: list) -> str:
+    """Neutral markdown disclosure section. Empty string for no blocks (default-OFF byte-identity).
+
+    Uses only neutral framing ("the evidence diverges", "evidence weight", "independent origins",
+    "weigh them yourself") — never a judgemental label. Shows EVERY side with its weight; the user judges.
+    """
+    if not blocks:
+        return ""
+    lines = [
+        "## Where sources diverge",
+        "",
+        "On the topics below the evidence does not agree. Each position is shown with its evidence "
+        "weight (origin-cluster weight-mass) and the number of independent origins behind it, plus its "
+        "cited sources. Both positions are shown as they stand in the evidence; weigh them yourself.",
+        "",
+    ]
+    for block in blocks:
+        lines.append(f"### On {block.subject}, the evidence diverges")
+        for index, side in enumerate(block.sides):
+            label = chr(ord("A") + index)
+            cited = ", ".join(side.evidence_ids) if side.evidence_ids else "—"
+            lines.append(
+                f"- **Position {label}** — evidence weight {side.weight_mass:.2f} across "
+                f"{side.independent_origin_count} independent origin(s). Cited: {cited}."
+            )
+        lines.append("")
+    return "\n".join(lines).rstrip() + "\n"
diff --git a/tests/polaris_graph/synthesis/test_both_sides_phase7.py b/tests/polaris_graph/synthesis/test_both_sides_phase7.py

@@ -0,0 +1,119 @@
+"""I-cred-007 (Phase 7) — neutral both-sides composer. Offline, deterministic, no network."""
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import pytest
+
+from src.polaris_graph.synthesis.both_sides import (
+    BothSidesBlock,
+    SidePosition,
+    bothsides_disclosure_enabled,
+    compose_both_sides,
+    render_both_sides,
+)
+
+_BANNED = ["fringe", "misinformation", "debunked", "conspiracy", "warning",
+           "unreliable", "false claim", "discredited"]
+
+
+def _edge(ccids, subject="vaccine safety", predicate="rate", source="numeric", severity="review"):
+    return type("E", (), {"claim_cluster_ids": tuple(ccids), "subject": subject,
+                          "predicate": predicate, "source": source, "severity": severity})()
+
+
+def _cwm(ccid, weight, origins):
+    return type("W", (), {"claim_cluster_id": ccid, "weight_mass": weight,
+                          "independent_origin_count": origins})()
+
+
+def _claim(ccid, eid, subject="vaccine safety", predicate="rate"):
+    return type("C", (), {"claim_cluster_id": ccid, "evidence_id": eid,
+                          "subject": subject, "predicate": predicate})()
+
+
+# ── AC-1 ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+def test_flag_default_off(monkeypatch):
+    monkeypatch.delenv("PG_SWEEP_BOTHSIDES_DISCLOSURE", raising=False)
+    assert bothsides_disclosure_enabled() is False
+
+
+@pytest.mark.parametrize("on", ["1", "true", "on", "yes", "TRUE"])
+def test_flag_on(monkeypatch, on):
+    monkeypatch.setenv("PG_SWEEP_BOTHSIDES_DISCLOSURE", on)
+    assert bothsides_disclosure_enabled() is True
+
+
+# ── AC-2: single edge, two sides ordered by weight DESC ──────────────────────
+def test_single_edge_two_sides_ordered_by_weight():
+    blocks = compose_both_sides(
+        [_edge(["cA", "cB"])],
+        [_cwm("cA", 0.9, 3), _cwm("cB", 0.2, 1)],
+        [_claim("cA", "e0"), _claim("cB", "e1")],
+    )
+    assert len(blocks) == 1
+    b = blocks[0]
+    assert len(b.sides) == 2
+    assert b.sides[0].claim_cluster_id == "cA"  # higher weight first
+    assert abs(b.sides[0].weight_mass - 0.9) < 1e-9 and b.sides[0].independent_origin_count == 3
+    assert abs(b.sides[1].weight_mass - 0.2) < 1e-9 and b.sides[1].independent_origin_count == 1
+    assert b.sides[0].evidence_ids == ("e0",)
+
+
+# ── AC-3: render([]) is byte-empty (default-OFF byte-identity) ───────────────
+def test_render_empty_is_byte_empty():
+    assert render_both_sides([]) == ""
+    assert compose_both_sides([], [], []) == []
+
+
+# ── AC-4: neutral language + both weights shown ──────────────────────────────
+def test_render_is_neutral_and_shows_both_weights():
+    text = render_both_sides(compose_both_sides(
+        [_edge(["cA", "cB"])],
+        [_cwm("cA", 0.9, 3), _cwm("cB", 0.2, 1)],
+        [_claim("cA", "e0"), _claim("cB", "e1")],
+    )).lower()
+    for banned in _BANNED:
+        assert banned not in text, f"neutral-language guardrail: '{banned}' must not appear"
+    assert "0.90" in text and "0.20" in text  # BOTH sides' weights are disclosed
+    assert "diverge" in text and "weigh" in text  # neutral frame, user judges
+
+
+# ── AC-5: a claim with no contradiction edge produces no block ───────────────
+def test_claim_with_no_edge_no_block():
+    assert compose_both_sides([], [_cwm("cA", 0.9, 3)],
+                              [_claim("cA", "e0"), _claim("cB", "e1")]) == []
+
+
+# ── AC-6: the low-weight side is shown, never dropped ────────────────────────
+def test_low_weight_side_not_dropped():
+    b = compose_both_sides(
+        [_edge(["cA", "cB"])],
+        [_cwm("cA", 0.99, 5), _cwm("cB", 0.01, 1)],
+        [_claim("cA", "e0"), _claim("cB", "e1")],
+    )[0]
+    assert len(b.sides) == 2
+    assert any(s.claim_cluster_id == "cB" for s in b.sides)  # low-weight side present
+    assert "0.01" in render_both_sides([b])
+
+
+# ── AC-7: missing weight_mass -> 0.0 / 0 fail-soft (no crash, no fabrication) ─
+def test_missing_weight_is_fail_soft():
+    b = compose_both_sides(
+        [_edge(["cA", "cB"])],
+        [_cwm("cA", 0.9, 3)],  # cB has NO weight entry
+        [_claim("cA", "e0"), _claim("cB", "e1")],
+    )[0]
+    side_b = next(s for s in b.sides if s.claim_cluster_id == "cB")
+    assert side_b.weight_mass == 0.0 and side_b.independent_origin_count == 0
+
+
+# ── AC-8: purity — inputs not mutated ────────────────────────────────────────
+def test_no_input_mutation():
+    weights = [_cwm("cA", 0.9, 3), _cwm("cB", 0.2, 1)]
+    claims = [_claim("cA", "e0"), _claim("cB", "e1")]
+    compose_both_sides([_edge(["cA", "cB"])], weights, claims)
+    assert weights[0].weight_mass == 0.9 and claims[0].evidence_id == "e0"
+
+
+def test_edge_with_one_cluster_is_skipped():
+    """An edge with fewer than two claim_cluster_ids produces no block (needs two positions)."""
+    assert compose_both_sides([_edge(["cA"])], [_cwm("cA", 0.9, 3)], [_claim("cA", "e0")]) == []
```

docs\full_power_polaris_architecture_2026_05_31.md:51:**Stage 9 — Composition + contradiction (surface conflicts, refuse to adjudicate).** Detects directional conflicts across deduped findings (one source asserts a clinical signal present, another absent, for the same endpoint+population) and **closes the shipped loop**: conflicts become a generation INPUT (Writer must disclose both sides, cite both spans, refuse to adjudicate) AND an evaluation GATE (the evaluator FAILS a report that hides a known directional conflict). Unverified "analyst voice" connective tissue is quarantined to a minimized, clearly-labeled Analysis block so it can never masquerade as a verified claim. **Model/tool:** Mirror (conflict detection) + Writer (conflict-as-input) + Judge (disclosure gate) + contradiction/refusal panel UI (task #454). **Fixes vs shipped (narrowed per Codex 2026-05-31):** NUMERIC contradictions are ALREADY fed into generation (`run_honest_sweep_r3.py:2613`) and disclosure-gated in the evaluator (PT08), so that path is not inert. The real gap full-power closes is QUALITATIVE conflicts — directional clinical disagreements written to `contradictions.json` but NOT yet fed to generation or bound to the evaluation gate. Full-power consumes the qualitative conflicts and adds the qualitative-disclosure gate.

docs\frontier_credibility_intelligence_2026_06_07.md:8:There is no deployed system today that does credibility-weighted, both-sides deep research well. The frontier products (OpenAI/Gemini/Perplexity Deep Research) are agentic and broad but treat credibility as prose narration or a clickable link list — never a disclosed weight. The scientific-evidence tools (Elicit, Consensus, scite, Semantic Scholar, Exa, STORM) mostly manufacture "credibility" by **restricting the corpus to peer-reviewed papers** — which is precisely the journal-only filter POLARIS is abandoning — and the ones that touch the open web (Exa, STORM) handle credibility badly. The formal evidence-synthesis frameworks (GRADE, GRADE-CERQual, Cochrane/Campbell, EFSA/OHAT weight-of-evidence, the Maryland SMS) get the *methodology* right — weight, never count — but assume trained human reviewers and curated studies, not an automated pipeline ingesting the whole web. And the credibility-aware RAG literature (RA-RAG, CAG, RAGRank) has working weighted-aggregation algorithms but keeps the weights internal and, critically, mostly **assumes source independence** — the one thing the contested hard case breaks.
docs\frontier_credibility_intelligence_2026_06_07.md:30:Each issue below covers the seven POLARIS dimensions: (a) source diversity vs filtering, (b) per-source credibility weighting + signals, (c) composition/synthesis weighted by credibility, (d) contested-topic both-sides handling (the vax case), (e) volume-vs-weight + source-independence/echo-chamber detection, (f) per-claim credibility disclosure. For each, what the frontier DOES, the SOTA best practice, and the OUTCOME (how well, known failures).
docs\frontier_credibility_intelligence_2026_06_07.md:42:**(d) Contested-topic / the vax case.** **All three FALSE-CONVERGE to one-sidedness, not false-balance.** DeepTRACE one-sidedness on debate queries: GPT-5(DR) 54.67% (best/lowest, yet still a majority), Perplexity(DR) 63.1%, Gemini(DR) 80.1% (second-worst). None has a documented weight-and-disclose policy for the vaccine-vs-antivaccine more-sources-but-lower-credibility case. Behavior is emergent from model training, not a transparent both-sides policy. **The failure mode is silent side-picking + under-support, which is arguably more dangerous than naive 50/50 because it is invisible.**
docs\credibility_adaptive_weighting_and_bothsides_recs_2026_06_08.md:1:# POLARIS Source-Credibility & Multi-Perspective Recommendations Report\n### Driving two revisions to `docs/credibility_weighted_sourcing_redesign_plan_2026_06_07.md` — LAYER 1 (scoring) and LAYER 6 (composition + UI)\n\n**Author:** Lead analyst (Claude). **Date:** 2026-06-08.\n**Inputs:** three research streams (per-question adaptive credibility weighting; neutral multi-perspective presentation; friendly UI/artifact patterns).\n**Status:** revision driver. Each layer below states what it **REPLACES** in the Codex-APPROVE'd 2026-06-07 plan, then the concrete mechanism, auditability, reliability, and POLARIS wiring.\n\n**Invariants preserved across both revisions** (these are not negotiable and the revisions do not weaken them): the LLM credibility-judge is **advisory only** — `strict_verify`'s six per-sentence checks (`provenance_generator.py:1156`) remain the binding faithfulness gate; every new layer is **flag-gated, default-OFF byte-identical**, fail-loud on missing inputs; weight is **evidence quality/tier, never headcount**; every displayed aggregate is **one click from the cited `[#ev:id:start-end]` span and its VERIFIED/PARTIAL verdict**; the credibility prior stays **self-computed and verifier-overridable** (no single external rater hardwired); independence-collapse (`synthesis/independence_collapse.py`) still runs before any weighted tally; the contested-topic adjudication **reuses the existing 4-role / voter-arbiter pipeline** (`roles/role_pipeline.py` + `honest_sweep_integration.py`), open-weight voters only — no parallel path is built.\n\n---\n\n## 1. LAYER 1 (scoring): adaptive per-question credibility-skill, replacing the fixed domain-rubric selector\n\n### 1.1 What this REPLACES\n\nThe 2026-06-07 plan's **Phase 2a/2b (L1)** selects one of **three fixed reliability rubrics** (clinical → RCT+peer-review+RoB; econ/policy → design-validity; qualitative → CERQual) keyed off the detected domain. That is still a small lookup table: domain → rubric. The operator constraint is explicit — **replace fixed domain rubrics** with a **generic, domain-agnostic credibility skill the LLM applies by reasoning per question**. Research stream #1's central finding is that the frontier (OpenAI, Gemini, Claude) has already moved this way, and that Perplexity's baked-in EEAT/domain-authority scoring is the closest-to-forbidden counter-example (gameable, popularity-biased, ~60% Google-overlap). We copy the reasoned-generic camp.\n\nThe revision: **domain stops being a selector and becomes context that primes one generic skill.** There is exactly one credibility skill; the detected `scope_template` domain is passed in as a hint the skill reasons over ("this is a clinical efficacy question, so weight trial design and RoB heavily"), not a branch that swaps rubrics. This scales to 10,000+ fields with zero per-field config.\n\n### 1.2 The exact mechanism — credibility-skill / guardrail prompt × (reliability × relevance)\n\n**Step A — deterministic signals (POLARIS produces these; unchanged substrate).** `authority_model.score_source_authority` and `tier_classifier` already emit, per source, the field-agnostic primitives: `authority_score [0,1]`, `source_class`, `corroboration_count` (independent-host agreement), `authority_confidence`, `signal_scores` (the A–E sub-scores), plus `junk_class` / `predatory_oa` (`source_class.py:71-89`). Independence-collapse (`independence_collapse.py`) emits `origin_cluster_id` + canonical-origin designation + copy flag. **None of this is replaced.** These are the inspectable, host-name-free, self-computed inputs (LAW VI: zero host literals in code).\n\n**Step B — the credibility skill consumes those signals and weights them per question.** A new pure prompt module, `authority/credibility_skill.py`, runs a **JudgeRank-style 3-step decomposition** (arXiv 2411.00142) — chosen because each step is inspectable text and is itself the audit template:\n\n1. **Query analysis** — identify what THIS question actually needs (the claim type, what would count as strong evidence for it).\n2. **Source analysis** — for each candidate source, a query-AWARE assessment applying **generic SIFT + lateral-reading + provenance heuristics**, NOT a domain table. The skill's instruction block encodes the domain-agnostic primacy heuristics that are OpenAI's own deep-research pattern: *prefer the primary/official source over an aggregator or SEO blog; prefer the original paper over a survey/secondary summary; corroborate laterally (does independent coverage agree); weigh source incentives/track record; downgrade stale-but-authoritative and retracted/superseded* (the latter wires to the existing `supersession.py` Phase 3 signal).\n3. **Two-axis judgment with rationale** — emit, per source, **RELIABILITY × RELEVANCE** (the EFSA/OHAT weight-of-evidence two-axis, which POLARIS currently conflates into one tier): reliability = internal validity/method given what the skill read in the signals; relevance = directness to this specific question. The product is the per-question credibility weight. **Crucially, the skill is told its priors are the `authority_model` signals and that it may up- or down-weight them with a stated reason** — it does not invent authority from nothing, and it cannot silently override `authority_confidence=LOW` into a fabricated HIGH (thin OpenAlex/ROR signal stays honestly LOW).\n\n**Output schema (machine-parseable, bound to the schema discipline already in §8.3.9):** per source — `{reliability_score, relevance_score, credibility_weight, rationale_string, signals_cited:[...]}`. The weight is **a visible, revisable rationale string, never a hidden scalar and never a fine-tuned-in behavior** (this is why we reject the CAG fine-tune approach from stream #1: opaque learned weights are exactly the auditability failure POLARIS differentiates against — borrow CAG's *evidence* that credibility-conditioning gives noise robustness, and its three generic dimensions of relevance/timeliness/reliability, but implement them at inference time as a prompt-visible signal).\n\n### 1.3 How it stays AUDITABLE (auditable by construction, not bolted on)\n\nThe judgment IS a reasoning trace, so it is emitted verbatim and **bound to the same provenance substrate POLARIS already has**:\n\n- The per-source `credibility_weight` + `rationale_string` + `signals_cited` attach to the source's `AuthorityResult` as **additive fields** (mirroring how `signal_scores`, `junk_class`, `predatory_oa` are already additive side-outputs on the dataclass), emitted on rows in `tier_classifier.py`.\n- At claim time, the weight flows into the four Phase-1/Phase-8 disclosure fields on `SentenceVerification` (`credibility_weight`, `independent_origin_count`, `certainty_label`, `span_verdict`), so each verified sentence shows **which source was weighted how, and why**, one click from its `[#ev]` span.\n- Because the skill cites the deterministic `signals_cited` it reasoned from, the rationale is **checkable against the inputs** — a reviewer can confirm "preferred A over B because A is the primary trial-registry entry and B a secondary news summary" against the actual `source_class` values. The rationale is a **claim to verify, not ground truth** (post-hoc rationalization risk per stream #1) — so it is advisory and the binding gate stays `strict_verify`.\n\nThis is the §-1.1-compliant story: no metadata/count/string-presence signal, every weight traceable to a cited span and an inspectable reason.\n\n### 1.4 Reliability and where it fails (and the guardrail)\n\nStream #1 is blunt about the failure modes, and they bound the design: LLMs "treat all retrieved documents as equally valid" unless explicitly steered and over-rely on high-frequency claims (arXiv 2505.17762); AuthorityBench (2603.25092) shows authority perception is **inconsistent across domains and highly prompt-sensitive**, struggles with false authority, and exhibits position/verbosity/self-preference bias. Therefore:\n\n- **The skill is ADVISORY to ranking/selection, never the faithfulness gate.** It changes *which rows are billed/weighted*, not *whether a sentence verifies its span*. `strict_verify`, 4-role/two-family segregation, and the independent `corpus_approval_gate` tier-distribution backstop all still run sequentially.\n- **Bias mitigations baked into the prompt:** score rationale-first then number; randomize candidate order to blunt position bias; run pointwise (per-source) to avoid listwise permutation instability.\n- **Offline validation before trust:** the chosen judge model+prompt is validated on an **AuthorityBench-style harness** (authority-PERCEPTION only, per the §6a no-overstatement correction — not as a volume-vulnerability benchmark) plus the existing vax adversarial fixture, before it is allowed on the shipping path. Calibration (Brier/ECE) on the emitted weights runs in the existing Phase 11 harness.\n- **Capture resistance:** multi-signal, self-computed, verifier-overridable — no NewsGuard/MBFC/Ad Fontes verdict is hardwired as ground truth (the FTC-capture risk).\n\n### 1.5 The honest gap + exactly what POLARIS builds for L1\n\n**HAVE:** deterministic authority signals (`authority_model`, `tier_classifier`), the additive `AuthorityResult`/`SentenceVerification` schema, independence-collapse, `scope_templates` domain detection, the JSON-verdict schema discipline.\n**MISSING:** the generic per-question credibility skill itself, and the second (relevance) axis.\n**BUILD (revision to Phase 2a/2b):**\n1. `authority/credibility_skill.py` — the pure 3-step (query→source→two-axis-judgment) prompt module emitting `{reliability, relevance, credibility_weight, rationale, signals_cited}`. Domain is an input *hint*, not a rubric switch. (Replaces the fixed-rubric selector in `credibility_prior.py`.)\n2. Add `relevance_score` (and the rationale fields) to `AuthorityResult` (`source_class.py:75`); emit on rows in `tier_classifier.py`.\n3. Wire the skill's weight into the L5 weight-mass tally and the L7 disclosure fields — advisory input, not a gate.\n4. Flag-gated default-OFF byte-identical; OFF = the legacy single-scalar path, byte-for-byte.\n\n---\n\n## 2. LAYER 6 (composition + UI): neutral multi-perspective + transparent evidence-weight artifact, replacing the forewarning/fringe framing\n\n### 2.1 What this REPLACES\n\nThe 2026-06-07 plan's **Phase 7 (L6)** composes contested claims as "consensus at high weight + minority attributed at low weight **with explicit forewarning**, medical-misinfo **low-weight/fringe**, ABSTAIN over fabricated balance." The operator directive is to **replace the forewarning/fringe framing** with a **neutral multi-perspective presentation where competing world-views are shown as legitimate, each carrying its real (possibly asymmetric) evidence weight, and the user judges** — no bias, no stamps, no forewarning prose.\n\n### 2.2 The hard tension, named and resolved (do not skip this)\n\nThere is a real conflict between two binding constraints, and both sides have a lethal failure mode:\n\n- The operator wants **no fringe/forewarning stamp, all sides legitimate, no bias.**\n- The **clinical-safety invariant #5** (binding, preserved) plus Dixon-Clarke 2013 (PubMed 23193194, measured harm: falsely-balanced vaccine reporting *reduced* perceived safety and vaccination intent), Wikipedia FRINGE, and §-1.1 all say **equal treatment of unequal evidence is itself bias** and is "lethal in clinical." I am not authorized to drop invariant #5.\n\n**The reconciliation — handed to us nearly verbatim by all three streams: replace the LABEL with the BASIS.** Wikipedia NPOV's "neutral *editing*, not neutral *content*"; GRADE's "show the basis, let the user infer"; the no-warning rule from stream #2 is satisfiable **if and only if the criteria behind any weight are displayed**. So:\n\n- The **system** stamps nothing — no "fringe," no "debunked," no forewarning sentence. That is the neutrality.\n- The **evidence weight** carries the (often asymmetric) truth, rendered as a visible **per-perspective evidence-basis panel** the user reads and judges. The asymmetry — *14 RCTs + 3 systematic reviews [High]* vs *2 case reports + mechanistic argument [Very Low]* — becomes **visible in the artifact** instead of **asserted in a stamp**. The user infers; the system does not editorialize.\n- "Legitimate" means **shown with its real (possibly low) weight and one-click drill-down to span + verdict** — NOT "shown as equally supported." A genuine world-view dispute with no empirical consensus (values, forecasting) shows steelmanned sides at honest parity; an empirical dispute with consensus shows the real weight distribution.\n- The medical-misinfo case is handled **without the banned word**: its panel is simply **near-empty of independent high-tier basis**, and where there is no independent consensus the claim **ABSTAINs** ("contested; no independent consensus" — reusing existing refuse/unresolved behavior). This preserves invariant #5's *substance* (not normalized as an equal side) while dropping the stamp.\n\nThis is neutral AND anti-false-balance AND §-1.1-safe simultaneously — the operator's "let the user judge" satisfied by *showing the basis*, not by *equalizing the boxes*.\n\n### 2.3 The exact composition mechanism\n\nPer question, the composition path first **diagnoses the contestation type** (this IS the adaptive guardrail, copied from Anthropic's even-handedness "lack-of-consensus" discriminator + OpenAI's seek-the-truth-together):\n\n- **empirical-with-consensus** (vaccines, climate) → due-weight: each side shown, weight proportional to verified-evidence quality; the asymmetry is the message, carried by the basis panel.\n- **genuine-uncertainty** (open scientific questions) → separate *supported* from *open*; sides at honest parity.\n- **values dispute** (politics, ethics) → **steelman each legitimate view** (Ideological Turing Test, neutral terminology, no verdict); no evidence-weight asymmetry asserted because there is no due weight to defer to.\n- **forecasting** (AI-and-jobs) → scenario spread, projective not factual.\n\nEach perspective is gathered through its **own retrieval lens** (MODS-style per-perspective retrieval + citation, arXiv 2502.00322 — raw LLMs silently drop minority views; per-perspective retrieval prevents the drop), then composed via the **existing 4-role / voter-arbiter agreement** (cross-lineage, open-weight voters — the bridging/balanced-panel analog) — **not a new adjudication path**. Reranking-for-balance (arXiv 2506.15925) selects the most balanced faithful candidate, because direct just-prompt-balanced generation empirically skews. **The weight attached to each perspective is evidence QUALITY × independent-origin count, never document count** — else we rebuild Ground News's source-count bias inside the summarizer.\n\n### 2.4 The friendly UI artifact — design\n\nBuilt on the **components that already exist** (#744 citation chip + hover source card, #745 per-claim verdict chip, #747 Proof Replay split-view, #757 report page, #758 claim-anchored compare view) — not designed from scratch.\n\n**The artifact: a claim-anchored "Perspectives" panel** that opens from any contested sentence (reusing the compare-view host), containing per legitimate perspective:\n\n1. **A neutral position header** — "Position held by [who], with this evidence behind it" — no "fringe"/"warning"/"debunked". A steelmanned one-line statement of the view in neutral terms.\n2. **An evidence-basis sub-panel (GRADE-style, the load-bearing element):** the study types / source tiers / independent-origin count behind that perspective, rendered as **frequencies, not a percentage or a lone dot** — "*8 of n: RCTs + systematic reviews [High certainty]*" vs "*2 of n: case reports + mechanistic argument [Very Low]*". The certainty label is acceptable **only because its downgrade criteria are shown** (study design / consistency / directness / independence). This makes the asymmetry self-evident without a stamp.\n3. **Scite-style polarity badges** (supporting / contrasting / contextualizing) on each cited source — **neutral hue + icon + text label, never color alone** (colorblind safety; red=contrasting reads as red=wrong and biases toward consensus — explicitly avoided).\n4. **Drill-down:** every badge, every basis count, every panel is **one click from the raw `[#ev]` span and its VERIFIED/PARTIAL verdict** — the Scite "self-correcting" property: a mis-classified badge is exposed by the citing sentence sitting right behind it, and a meter without drill-down would violate the §-1.1 metadata-audit ban.\n\n**Panel sizing defeats false balance structurally, not with a caveat:** panels are **sized/annotated by real verified-evidence weight**, not equal-width — because equal real estate reads as equal credibility (the false-balance trap), and a caveat is empirically insufficient (Effectiviology / false-balance literature). The asymmetry is *in the layout and the basis panel*, not asserted in prose.\n\n**Three named anti-patterns explicitly rejected** (all from the streams, all as negative templates):\n- **Ground News source-count / coverage bar** — measures who-is-saying-this (volume), not evidence weight; §-1.1 bans source counts as quality signals. If a composition strip is shown at all, its axis is **evidence tier / source type**, never ideology or headcount, and it is kept visually separate from the weight panel so "many sources" never reads as "true."\n- **Bare confidence/credibility score (% or traffic-light dot)** — the best-documented HARM pattern: overconfident displays (80% shown / 70% accurate) pushed AI-advice adoption 57%→69.6%, 64% of users mis-judged calibration, and in a 2025 breast-cancer CDSS high confidence *reduced* diagnostic accuracy via overreliance. POLARIS's honest replacement is the per-sentence VERIFIED/PARTIAL verdict against a real span — never a glanceable dot.\n- **Symmetric 50/50 equal-box presentation** — manufactures false balance; the Dixon-Clarke measured harm.\n\n### 2.5 The honest gap + exactly what POLARIS builds for L6\n\n**HAVE:** the disclosure substrate (per-sentence `[#ev]` tokens, `strict_verify` verdict ladder, `SentenceVerification` additive fields), the existing 4-role/voter-arbiter agreement, independence-collapse for origin-count, and the full UI component kit (citation chip, verdict chip, Proof Replay, compare view).\n**MISSING:** the contestation-type classifier, per-perspective retrieval + composition that defeats false balance by weight, and the Perspectives artifact rendering basis panels.\n**BUILD (revision to Phase 7):**\n1. A **contestation-type classifier** (empirical-consensus / genuine-uncertainty / values / forecasting) priming the composition rule — replaces the fixed forewarning+fringe rule.\n2. **Per-perspective retrieval + balance-rerank composition** over the post-collapse origins, weighting each perspective by verified-evidence quality × independent-origin count (not count).\n3. A **steelman + GRADE-style evidence-basis renderer** feeding a new **claim-anchored "Perspectives" panel** in the compare-view host: neutral headers, frequency-framed basis sub-panels, Scite-style neutral polarity badges, full span-verdict drill-down, weight-proportional sizing.\n4. Validated with a **paired-prompt neutrality eval** (Anthropic's open-sourced political-neutrality harness, adapted so it does NOT reward equal treatment of unequal evidence) + the vax adversarial fixture (asserts the asymmetry renders, no stamp, no 50/50).\n5. Flag-gated default-OFF byte-identical; ABSTAIN reuses existing refuse/unresolved behavior; forewarning prose removed, replaced by the basis panel.\n\n---\n\n## 3. ## 1. GOAL + NON-NEGOTIABLES

### 1.1 Goal

Turn POLARIS from a **count-and-tier-threshold** sourcing pipeline into a **credibility-WEIGHTED, independence-aware, per-claim-disclosed** one — the union that no deployed system offers (§3): a disclosed credibility weight that (a) is domain-conditional, (b) discounts non-independent corroboration *before* aggregation, and (c) actually drives composition and is shown per claim. We extend POLARIS's existing hard substrate — per-sentence `[#ev:id:start-end]` tokens + `strict_verify` + zero-verified-abort — from *provenance disclosure* to *provenance + weight + independent-origin-count + certainty disclosure*.

### 1.2 Non-negotiables (these override every design choice below)

1. **Faithfulness gates are preserved, never weakened.** The four gates stay intact and any verifier work is **additive-only**:
   - **strict_verify** (`provenance_generator.py:1156` `verify_sentence_provenance`) — six per-sentence checks (evidence-pool membership, span bounds, numeric match, ≥2 content-word overlap, trial-name, entailment). New work *adds* checks on top (§6c-7); it never relaxes one of the six.
   - **4-role / two-family segregation** (`check_family_segregation`, enforced e.g. `semantic_conflict_detector.py:346`) — untouched. Generator and evaluator stay cross-lineage.
   - **provenance token grammar** `[#ev:id:start-end]` — unchanged. New fields are *side-outputs* on `SentenceVerification`, never inputs to the verdict.
   - **corpus_approval_gate** (`corpus_approval_gate.py`, FX-05) — stays an **independent downstream backstop**. Weight-based adequacy does NOT bypass it; both gates run sequentially.
2. **No silent downgrade (LAW II + operator directive 2026-06-04).** Every new layer ships behind a flag, **default-OFF byte-identical**, fail-loud when its inputs are missing. Capability caps are surfaced and per-cap approved, never silently applied.
3. **Domain-aware, not a global hierarchy (§4 ISSUE 4 — "there is no universal evidence hierarchy").** Clinical weights RCT+peer-review+RoB; econ/policy weights design-validity over venue (the Nobel-validated shift — a strong NBER natural experiment must not rank below a weak peer-reviewed cross-section); qualitative weights coherence/adequacy. Domain is detected off the existing `scope_templates`.
4. **Sovereign + capture-resistant.** `authority_model.py` is already host-name-free, data-driven (LAW VI — "ZERO host names in code"). The credibility prior stays **multi-signal, self-computed, and OVERRIDABLE by the claim-level verifier** — no single external rater (NewsGuard/MBFC/Ad Fontes) hardwired as ground truth (the FTC-capture risk in §4 ISSUE 3).
5. **Clinical-safety weighting invariant (task §6 + §6c-8).** Web/news *volume* must never outweigh the **absence of clinical evidence**; medical/health misinformation is disclosed as **low-weight / fringe**, explicitly NOT normalized as an equal "side." Honest failure mode is **ABSTAIN** ("contested; no independent consensus"), never a fabricated balanced verdict.
6. **Weight beats count, and independence is collapsed before the vote** — the through-line of the whole source doc.

---

## 2. TARGET ARCHITECTURE — the 8 layers mapped onto our concrete files

The source doc frames a six-stage flow `retrieve → score → independence-collapse → aggregate → compose → disclose`. §6c **extends** this with three net-new layers (temporal/supersession, claim-graph-before-voting, retrieval dissent-recall) and four cross-cutting strengtheners (article+claim scoring, independence-beyond-TFIDF, calibration/audit, additive verifier). The table below is the full §6c-aware target; **REUSE** = existing code we re-wire, **BUILD** = genuinely new.

| # | Layer (flow stage) | What it does | REUSE (existing file:anchor) | BUILD (new) |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| L0 | **Retrieve broadly + dissent-recall** (§6c-6) | All-source-type retrieval; *actively seek* the best minority-side / contrary evidence; stratify by source-type | `live_retriever.py` retrieval lanes; subquery-reserve diversity pass `evidence_selector.py:552-660` (`_reserve_subqueries:602`); domain soft-cap `:661-704` (`_apply_domain_cap`); selection-time passes `:1513-1542` | dissent-recall sub-query expansion + source-type stratification quota (net-new, upstream of scoring) |
| L1 | **Score — two-axis, domain-conditional, article+claim** (§4 L1 + §6c-1) | Reliability × Relevance, primary axis chosen by domain; article-level (author/venue/method/funding/date/corrections) AND claim-specific relevance, not just host prior | `authority_model.py` signals A–E (scalar blend); `tier_classifier.py:135-142` additive fields `authority_score`/`corroboration_count`/`authority_confidence`; `scope_templates/` for domain | second **relevance** axis; domain-conditional rubric selector; article-level + claim-level decomposition (real BUILD — current blend is one field-agnostic scalar) |
| L2 | **Temporal / supersession** (§6c-2) | Downgrade stale-but-authoritative evidence (old guidelines, superseded regs/datasets, retracted/corrected) even when the source is high-authority | Signal E recency `recency.py` / `authority_model.py:138-145`; `is_retracted` in journal sidecar `journal_only_filter.py:237` | supersession rules (guideline/reg/dataset version), retraction → **hard** penalty surfaced per claim |
| L3 | **Independence-collapse — beyond near-duplicate** (§4 L2 + §6c-4) | Collapse content-copying / syndication / common-ownership / common-funding / shared-authorship / citation-chain / paraphrase clusters to ~1 origin BEFORE any weighted vote | `corroboration.py` eTLD+1 PSL host-collapse (`count_independent_hosts`, `registrable_domain`); `finding_dedup.py` already clusters by finding + counts independent registrable-domains (`dedup_by_finding`, host-based) | TF-IDF cosine ≥0.85 **content-copy detector** + ownership/funding/authorship signals on top of the host primitive (real BUILD — current collapse is host-based only) |
| L4 | **Claim-graph BEFORE aggregation** (§6c-3, NEW sub-layer) | atomic-claim extraction → normalization → stance clustering → contradiction/refutation detection → span entailment, so equivalent claims are clustered before any vote | `finding_dedup.py` numeric-finding clustering (seed, clinical-numeric only); `semantic_conflict_detector.py` + `qualitative_conflict_detector.py` + numeric `contradiction_detector.py` (stance/contradiction seeds); entailment path in `verify_sentence_provenance` | field-agnostic atomic-claim extractor + normalization + stance-cluster graph (real BUILD — finding_dedup is numeric-only and inert on non-clinical) |
| L5 | **Aggregate by weight, auditable non-averaging** (§4 L3) | Weighted Majority Voting over post-collapse independent origins; inverse-variance for quantitative; GRADE "lowest-among-critical" for multi-part certainty | `plan_sufficiency_gate.py` already uses `authority_score` as a numeric GATE (`:50`, `:301`) | replace COUNT aggregation (`plan_sufficiency_gate.py:313` `covered_count >= target`; journal `DEFAULT_MIN_DISTINCT_JOURNALS=12` `journal_only_filter.py:531`) with **origin-cluster weight-mass** (one weight per independent-origin cluster; copied rows cannot inflate mass — Phase 6 invariant) |
| L6 | **Contested-topic composition — weight-and-disclose-with-forewarning** (§4 L4 + §6c-8 multi-position) | Consensus side at high weight AND minority **attributed** at low weight, with explicit **forewarning** (the N=887 finding: forewarning works, outnumbering does not). Multi-position, not binary. Medical misinfo = low-weight/fringe. ABSTAIN over fabricated balance | cross-lineage multi-judge agreement via the EXISTING 4-role adjudication — integration point `roles/role_pipeline.py` + `honest_sweep_integration.py` (REUSE, do NOT build a parallel adjudication path); existing refuse/unresolved behavior; retraction flag | forewarning composition rule + multi-position (>2 side) disclosure policy + clinical-fringe down-weight |
| L7 | **Per-claim disclosure** (§4 L5 + §6c-1 claim-level) | Each verified sentence carries {span-verdict, credibility_weight, independent_origin_count, certainty_label}; rendered in bibliography; "Proof Replay" SUPPORTS-not-EXISTS UX | `SentenceVerification` additive-field precedent (`soft_warnings` `:427`, `judge_error` `:433`); `resolve_provenance_to_citations` `:1881` render point | four optional fields + bibliography render + certainty-label scoring fn |
| L8 | **Additive verifier strengthening** (§6c-7) | NLI/QA entailment + unit/table/quantity checks + contradiction-sensitive verification **ON TOP of** strict_verify's six (never weakening) | existing NLI advisory path; `semantic_conflict_detector.py`; numeric checks in `verify_sentence_provenance` | wire the advisory NLI/contradiction checks as additive fail-closed gates (flag-gated, ON-mode only) |
| Lx | **Calibration + audit** (§6c-5) + **adversarial benchmark** (§4 L6) | Brier/ECE reliability curves on the weights; blinded per-claim faithfulness eval; ablations per layer; SourceBench/DeepTRACE/ReportBench suites | existing manifest telemetry; `outputs/audits/` §-1.1 harness | calibration metric script + adversarial vax fixture + benchmark harness (test infra, not pipeline) |

**Reuse vs build, in one honest sentence each:**
- **`authority_model.py`** blends A–E into ONE field-agnostic scalar — the second (relevance) axis + domain conditioning is a real BUILD, not a rewire.
- **`finding_dedup.py` / `corroboration.py`** give us the independent-origin PRIMITIVE, but **host-based** only; §6c-4 content-copy detection is a BUILD on top.
- **`SentenceVerification` + `resolve_provenance_to_citations`** are the disclosure substrate — additive fields, lowest-risk first phase.
- **`plan_sufficiency_gate.py`** already treats `authority_score` as a numeric gate — converting its COUNT aggregation to WEIGHT-MASS is a small, surgical re-wire.

| L5 weighted aggregate | COUNT thresholds (`plan_sufficiency_gate.py:313`); journal COUNT floor (`journal_only_filter.py:531,596`) | origin-cluster weight-mass = Σ over origin clusters of `authority_score(canonical_origin)` (one mass per `origin_cluster_id` = its canonical origin's authority; derivative copies contribute zero; NO row-level term, NO max-over-copies — Phase 6 invariant) | replace `covered_count >= target` with `weight_mass >= weight_target` (`plan_sufficiency_gate.py:312-317`); add `assess_journal_only_adequacy` weight path (`journal_only_filter.py:543-607`); consumes L3 `origin_cluster_id` |
| L6 forewarning compose | refuse/unresolved; 4-role agreement | weight-and-disclose-with-forewarning; multi-position; clinical-fringe | new composition rule in the generator's contested-claim path; forewarning string injected via `soft_warnings` channel |
| L7 per-claim disclose | `SentenceVerification` fields; bibliography render | 4 new optional fields + render | add `span_verdict`/`credibility_weight`/`independent_origin_count`/`certainty_label` to `SentenceVerification` (`provenance_generator.py:419-433`); extend bibliography dict (`:1897-1903`) |
| L8 additive verifier | strict_verify six checks; advisory NLI | NLI/unit/contradiction as additive fail-closed gates | new `additive_verifiers.py` invoked AFTER the six checks in `verify_sentence_provenance`; ON-mode flag-gated, never relaxes the six |
| Lx calibration/bench | manifest telemetry; §-1.1 harness | Brier/ECE + ablations + vax fixture + suites | new `tests/fixtures/credibility/` + `scripts/credibility_calibration.py`; benchmark harness for §6b suites |

**§6a corrections honored (no overstatement):** AuthorityBench is cited only as an authority-PERCEPTION benchmark, NOT a volume-vulnerability benchmark. DeepTRACE Perplexity numbers are framed "low minimum-cover / weak grounding," not "94.5% decorative." RA-RAG is the aggregation primitive AFTER independence-collapse, not a solution to it. The "79%→17% tool-call collapse" stat is replaced by the supportable "39–77% factual accuracy / ~42% average fact-check drop." CAG is EMNLP 2024 and its labels are relevance/timeliness, not source authority. RAGRank is inspiration (CTI PoC), not a validated web echo detector. Community-Notes/Elicit stats are flagged as needing their own primary citations before being treated as settled.
